cancel_building_effect  = {
        if = {
                limit = {
                        NOT = { has_variable = total_invested_building }
                        any_scope_building = {
                                is_building_type = building_investment_industry
                        }
                }
                every_scope_state = { 
                        limit = { has_building = building_investment_industry}
                        remove_building = building_investment_industry 
                }
                trigger_event = { id = fi_dividend_collector.4 }
        }
        else_if = {
                limit = { NOT = { has_variable = total_invested_building } }
        }
        else_if = {
                limit = {
                        var:total_invested_building < 1
                }
                capital = { remove_building = building_investment_industry }
                remove_variable = total_invested_building
                trigger_event = { id = fi_dividend_collector.4 }
        }
        else_if = {
                limit = { var:total_invested_building > 10000 }
        }
        else = {
                trigger_event = { id = fi_dividend_collector.4 }
                capital = { remove_building =  building_investment_industry 
                        switch = {
                                trigger = owner.var:total_invested_building
1 = {create_building = {building = building_investment_industry level = 1}}
